<span key="6fc4387a8b2f440daa08613f8835ffe9"><span offset-key="6fc4387a8b2f440daa08613f8835ffe9:0">split</span></span>

<span key="8e3865ad36614ce9b1a1b8430af4ab6c"><span offset-key="8e3865ad36614ce9b1a1b8430af4ab6c:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="e24ada0da11849ecbb58d4a48ab4f05d"><span offset-key="e24ada0da11849ecbb58d4a48ab4f05d:0">Error</span></span>

<span key="dd7557a0fed14352bf7b137ffe5316ac">`Error`<span offset-key="dd7557a0fed14352bf7b137ffe5316ac:1"> objects are thrown when runtime errors occur. The </span>`Error`<span offset-key="dd7557a0fed14352bf7b137ffe5316ac:3"> object can also be used as a base object for user-defined exceptions. See below for standard built-in error types.</span></span>

## 

<span key="193beb15ac644527a6853c4ff6311ea9"><span offset-key="193beb15ac644527a6853c4ff6311ea9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error#description" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="16ba9722176a4793912648c729325531" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="360370e849c04864ba2fe75da06301a1"><span data-offset-key="360370e849c04864ba2fe75da06301a1:0">Description</span></span></span></a><span key="ea4221508d1d4e49b4c6ccdcc922a74d"><span offset-key="ea4221508d1d4e49b4c6ccdcc922a74d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="92f92bedc2ff42f0a0747ed5d581e448"><span offset-key="92f92bedc2ff42f0a0747ed5d581e448:0">Runtime errors result in new </span>`Error`<span offset-key="92f92bedc2ff42f0a0747ed5d581e448:2"> objects being created and thrown.</span></span>

### 

<span key="809e7d50bd674045b7e374404f35f549"><span offset-key="809e7d50bd674045b7e374404f35f549:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error#error_types" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="39ab66b4786249288ef1055b2919d861" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="631507647d2d40c4b1d630d3defa65a2"><span data-offset-key="631507647d2d40c4b1d630d3defa65a2:0">Error types</span></span></span></a><span key="27bf1d4f7c484208a20f2a5b2245c127"><span offset-key="27bf1d4f7c484208a20f2a5b2245c127:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="fd50923760624c26ba0f570d78bc26b1"><span offset-key="fd50923760624c26ba0f570d78bc26b1:0">Besides the generic </span>`Error`<span offset-key="fd50923760624c26ba0f570d78bc26b1:2"> constructor, there are other core error constructors in JavaScript. For client-side exceptions, see </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Guide/Control_flow_and_error_handling#exception_handling_statements" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="83654685df824f52a42f5ee3c832bd98" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="38a760ca766e4e30a22ed1af4aa709b7"><span data-offset-key="38a760ca766e4e30a22ed1af4aa709b7:0">Exception handling statements</span></span></span></a><span key="5ec7e15532ee407a9da2ed8ace424e1f"><span offset-key="5ec7e15532ee407a9da2ed8ace424e1f:0">.</span></span>

<span key="8ab49a49a1c64937b6712ea99ccfddb0"><span offset-key="8ab49a49a1c64937b6712ea99ccfddb0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/EvalError" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="e95cbc6b56704d6e96e2474bd463516c" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="ddca6a065aca470cab0f8aa147e4886d"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="ddca6a065aca470cab0f8aa147e4886d:0">EvalError</code></span></span></a><span key="664a3df2b61b4c60a6337cb0f24ff745"><span offset-key="664a3df2b61b4c60a6337cb0f24ff745:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="0d2131330b2541a7b42843306a8616f3"><span offset-key="0d2131330b2541a7b42843306a8616f3:0">Creates an instance representing an error that occurs regarding the global function </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/eval" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="ef3930af3d4540d087381a572d46c356" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="d01b596fb50d421bbd073feccadbf829"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="d01b596fb50d421bbd073feccadbf829:0">eval()</code></span></span></a><span key="bbff9f8f967c4940b1d2924ef1a9ed72"><span offset-key="bbff9f8f967c4940b1d2924ef1a9ed72:0">.</span></span>

<span key="4d463393d2de453b917030247210ae11"><span offset-key="4d463393d2de453b917030247210ae11:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/RangeError" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="49c19223e3354a0f9bed441587eeb0f3" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="22b0eb39e72342fcb42c52153e5da875"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="22b0eb39e72342fcb42c52153e5da875:0">RangeError</code></span></span></a><span key="1ad7a882127b41cab25d58139549869a"><span offset-key="1ad7a882127b41cab25d58139549869a:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="dc5be0239477498c9a516bd062d5fb3b"><span offset-key="dc5be0239477498c9a516bd062d5fb3b:0">Creates an instance representing an error that occurs when a numeric variable or parameter is outside of its valid range.</span></span>

<span key="83f61ac1a31a4551a5c77e5d136f01f4"><span offset-key="83f61ac1a31a4551a5c77e5d136f01f4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/ReferenceError" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="b3053f8de6e84377b06f83256d2b2639" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="15fc8cadce7f45bbabf063916de990fb"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="15fc8cadce7f45bbabf063916de990fb:0">ReferenceError</code></span></span></a><span key="eefb1ab6d0ab45ac9f541661b2b3bae8"><span offset-key="eefb1ab6d0ab45ac9f541661b2b3bae8:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="a644b5e7dabc456ba8a44ea109a994df"><span offset-key="a644b5e7dabc456ba8a44ea109a994df:0">Creates an instance representing an error that occurs when de-referencing an invalid reference.</span></span>

<span key="11bdfe55760c4b159c9c185196fc5b67"><span offset-key="11bdfe55760c4b159c9c185196fc5b67:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/SyntaxError" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="dd541b7e050449fa84a0662941f980bb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="d081b4154b394c32918a1624905d3985"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="d081b4154b394c32918a1624905d3985:0">SyntaxError</code></span></span></a><span key="5e466f12c96249d5bb8f692daa694014"><span offset-key="5e466f12c96249d5bb8f692daa694014:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="13e0967e32414f50a93202b608f67ae6"><span offset-key="13e0967e32414f50a93202b608f67ae6:0">Creates an instance representing a syntax error.</span></span>

<span key="ef1e89c5ce5b4599a998b1794b874311"><span offset-key="ef1e89c5ce5b4599a998b1794b874311:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/TypeError" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f95005ef0c364635b45d20f89e9bdf8a" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="2e27f64fbb5a41c5b97cc50623600170"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="2e27f64fbb5a41c5b97cc50623600170:0">TypeError</code></span></span></a><span key="8e7407b482f442e3b10f25cafcf93fd2"><span offset-key="8e7407b482f442e3b10f25cafcf93fd2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="638bea476dfd4090ad7a97f27d40ecca"><span offset-key="638bea476dfd4090ad7a97f27d40ecca:0">Creates an instance representing an error that occurs when a variable or parameter is not of a valid type.</span></span>

<span key="4e71fb6fc2a74a18967532b72118c0be"><span offset-key="4e71fb6fc2a74a18967532b72118c0be:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/URIError" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="3d8920fea69c4ab58552474468316c33" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="6358b06ba34d4b658dfb41b918593386"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="6358b06ba34d4b658dfb41b918593386:0">URIError</code></span></span></a><span key="939ada13b87d47178002454f18e1201d"><span offset-key="939ada13b87d47178002454f18e1201d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="9c487cad5fe64bd2a8136b044c5c3469"><span offset-key="9c487cad5fe64bd2a8136b044c5c3469:0">Creates an instance representing an error that occurs when </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/encodeURI" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="4260b5a4c6014abdbdcdd31a204db3ea" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="2a91eb76f453434e95f45e07da408fac"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="2a91eb76f453434e95f45e07da408fac:0">encodeURI()</code></span></span></a><span key="a24bd385a7c5484b99f012bcfc525934"><span offset-key="a24bd385a7c5484b99f012bcfc525934:0"> or </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/decodeURI" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="efb4e32b11ef411a9e7b48f9476894e4" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="2033c9b402ac42488ae7f39f5074ab38"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="2033c9b402ac42488ae7f39f5074ab38:0">decodeURI()</code></span></span></a><span key="9c6939337399451a8c130de0d7bd3841"><span offset-key="9c6939337399451a8c130de0d7bd3841:0"> are passed invalid parameters.</span></span>

<span key="16b657b0e34d4020be77577706624f0d"><span offset-key="16b657b0e34d4020be77577706624f0d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/AggregateError" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="0d300a43066542cfb7bdc6e8d65893c0" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="ea46edc178d841cb8cedbba460f91e81"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="ea46edc178d841cb8cedbba460f91e81:0">AggregateError</code></span></span></a><span key="5adbe20e30e84efe84abae1bdcb05713"><span offset-key="5adbe20e30e84efe84abae1bdcb05713:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="d6bf801f2de541edae331df9327e41e4"><span offset-key="d6bf801f2de541edae331df9327e41e4:0">Creates an instance representing several errors wrapped in a single error when multiple errors need to be reported by an operation, for example by </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Promise/any" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c413acd1190b4addbc5d32229b2755bb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="c0bed4bfac7743bf8bac2e70b22b9166"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="c0bed4bfac7743bf8bac2e70b22b9166:0">Promise.any()</code></span></span></a><span key="6b01a0d07f664078a9c38b5f33a61914"><span offset-key="6b01a0d07f664078a9c38b5f33a61914:0">.</span></span>

<span key="c4328052d5ec48019fda8643982cfb83"><span offset-key="c4328052d5ec48019fda8643982cfb83:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/InternalError" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8c800281c5774e10b3d89d5309c37809" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="8a615caa054e4513b0e7127751943738"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="8a615caa054e4513b0e7127751943738:0">InternalError</code></span></span></a><span key="b4572a9ef67d436e9f692f3df46c375b"><span offset-key="b4572a9ef67d436e9f692f3df46c375b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="1c0cfb48036648e381e56870c1d75657"><span offset-key="1c0cfb48036648e381e56870c1d75657:0">Creates an instance representing an error that occurs when an internal error in the JavaScript engine is thrown. E.g. "too much recursion".</span></span>

## 

<span key="2c2322ca8bd5455e811487d83015479b"><span offset-key="2c2322ca8bd5455e811487d83015479b:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error#constructor" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="8cbdc74d765c4d8c874186d59a19ff3d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="1a44f8a4461142d9b6ec1365d19f2b41"><span data-offset-key="1a44f8a4461142d9b6ec1365d19f2b41:0">Constructor</span></span></span></a><span key="c5d5a361fa55418db3b19ce2ab96f6e5"><span offset-key="c5d5a361fa55418db3b19ce2ab96f6e5:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="a1c85309ed09481fbe8f2bd23965b447"><span offset-key="a1c85309ed09481fbe8f2bd23965b447:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/Error" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="81c6f95576e74ad4a86e9270ecb42b50" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="b13da1194af94e08ba44ce51f2db1d07"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="b13da1194af94e08ba44ce51f2db1d07:0">Error()</code></span></span></a><span key="516b0904800641429104a1b05f57f7c6"><span offset-key="516b0904800641429104a1b05f57f7c6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="96ec9d4c2d7843039dd9ca430ce3357f"><span offset-key="96ec9d4c2d7843039dd9ca430ce3357f:0">Creates a new </span>`Error`<span offset-key="96ec9d4c2d7843039dd9ca430ce3357f:2"> object.</span></span>

## 

<span key="be0790e65371480590b0ec99827030f4"><span offset-key="be0790e65371480590b0ec99827030f4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error#static_methods" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f10a42619dae461c9056702880331aa8" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="a22c20b9bcac4b169473dfb621e2adc4"><span data-offset-key="a22c20b9bcac4b169473dfb621e2adc4:0">Static methods</span></span></span></a><span key="bdb3029e23424930b84340d845c4d255"><span offset-key="bdb3029e23424930b84340d845c4d255:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="9ff2ff59204c458b8032615898179f0e">`Error.captureStackTrace()`</span>

<span key="279f0cb76fa846ac8323daabb892d20b"><span offset-key="279f0cb76fa846ac8323daabb892d20b:0">A non-standard </span>**V8**<span offset-key="279f0cb76fa846ac8323daabb892d20b:2"> function that creates the </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/Stack" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f1f20f3ccdce4f989cfa6b1be07a17e5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="09a2c1f263bf42ddbcf48f34749d0039"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="09a2c1f263bf42ddbcf48f34749d0039:0">stack</code></span></span></a><span key="0c403c826565480fae2ced6f0f35ba35"><span offset-key="0c403c826565480fae2ced6f0f35ba35:0"> property on an Error instance.</span></span>

## 

<span key="02682fe829dd477d94ae7aff5be551c4"><span offset-key="02682fe829dd477d94ae7aff5be551c4:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error#instance_properties" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="bcb4a70c38764c0aaab472f3b561ce80" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="cf3665656c1e4d588c51405b006fcf8f"><span data-offset-key="cf3665656c1e4d588c51405b006fcf8f:0">Instance properties</span></span></span></a><span key="4fd9d14b598246a8870f22646f5016e6"><span offset-key="4fd9d14b598246a8870f22646f5016e6:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="779a26078da8401e81a89aeed12acb7d"><span offset-key="779a26078da8401e81a89aeed12acb7d:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/message" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="a3e8a6388df6495aace3a8c71612e997" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="8824535e69b44183a2b9fc4b8f987aeb"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="8824535e69b44183a2b9fc4b8f987aeb:0">Error.prototype.message</code></span></span></a><span key="048177c46eca420c855234ad61968ca2"><span offset-key="048177c46eca420c855234ad61968ca2:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="75e5374b3fda465b98dadb57f13fa31a"><span offset-key="75e5374b3fda465b98dadb57f13fa31a:0">Error message.</span></span>

<span key="005de4e14aa844e9a21ff9908d4ec023"><span offset-key="005de4e14aa844e9a21ff9908d4ec023:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/name" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="09be243a604b40b8905ddbd9932aeda5" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="e87f1279bd1646dfb98438e71d681346"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="e87f1279bd1646dfb98438e71d681346:0">Error.prototype.name</code></span></span></a><span key="5fe298170b3d4a54b85d9b5f598c3790"><span offset-key="5fe298170b3d4a54b85d9b5f598c3790:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="0d834fe0b030463484f4765211f03bc7"><span offset-key="0d834fe0b030463484f4765211f03bc7:0">Error name.</span></span>

<span key="a6c3b8992b06492fa5ae6d4f7e75c9c7">`Error.prototype.description`</span>

<span key="d0d3b506eca544d8bd2c730b72fe27a9"><span offset-key="d0d3b506eca544d8bd2c730b72fe27a9:0">A non-standard Microsoft property for the error description. Similar to </span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/message" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="d00f00338bcc4e1f8416b5df06fcb90d" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="29196a674db14e1b9e9a55c11e33460a"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="29196a674db14e1b9e9a55c11e33460a:0">message</code></span></span></a><span key="5d77696249b141ddb7157da94244a2d1"><span offset-key="5d77696249b141ddb7157da94244a2d1:0">.</span></span>

<span key="d46851e0584c49d582b31d512b804d60">`Error.prototype.number`</span>

<span key="60cd326973bc47beaf6d199813039cef"><span offset-key="60cd326973bc47beaf6d199813039cef:0">A non-standard Microsoft property for an error number.</span></span>

<span key="f7dbdd03576749ab8fe03ef932159b53"><span offset-key="f7dbdd03576749ab8fe03ef932159b53:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/fileName" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="fe5b068b4ae44000835661f63b9eb647" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="73532b1c7fbf4ed5a821bfd24ac6078f"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="73532b1c7fbf4ed5a821bfd24ac6078f:0">Error.prototype.fileName</code></span></span></a><span key="5f632cf2bcb648ad85d67ca1bd448598"><span offset-key="5f632cf2bcb648ad85d67ca1bd448598:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="88d9f3c2850d457aa1fc29db538ffbcd"><span offset-key="88d9f3c2850d457aa1fc29db538ffbcd:0">A non-standard Mozilla property for the path to the file that raised this error.</span></span>

<span key="449096bfb920466293dc21f758ed6d95"><span offset-key="449096bfb920466293dc21f758ed6d95:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/lineNumber" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="2fe574a890764a83997458ad04367292" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="3a482222d5f8454493f4b82622f4c7a0"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3a482222d5f8454493f4b82622f4c7a0:0">Error.prototype.lineNumber</code></span></span></a><span key="2713624142c14999be0a13acc4124abb"><span offset-key="2713624142c14999be0a13acc4124abb:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="cd68b288e3f146308a4359202261a6b5"><span offset-key="cd68b288e3f146308a4359202261a6b5:0">A non-standard Mozilla property for the line number in the file that raised this error.</span></span>

<span key="101827864ccf4ced81ea5c72b78682e0"><span offset-key="101827864ccf4ced81ea5c72b78682e0:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/columnNumber" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="846cec553d1e426eb942bcd9e22a2380" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="3328e56b365c47f0a6263ea49f5a2cd3"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="3328e56b365c47f0a6263ea49f5a2cd3:0">Error.prototype.columnNumber</code></span></span></a><span key="da2d602906524948a65ea82ad0234446"><span offset-key="da2d602906524948a65ea82ad0234446:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="83b557bd6c314e518ac543d4019ab567"><span offset-key="83b557bd6c314e518ac543d4019ab567:0">A non-standard Mozilla property for the column number in the line that raised this error.</span></span>

<span key="0ab2aca6b7d1485baf332d0123d7de6c"><span offset-key="0ab2aca6b7d1485baf332d0123d7de6c:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span><a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/JavaScript/Reference/Global_Objects/Error/Stack" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="1248713060904276927fd1cd12c22c45" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="987f6d7645fe40e99accc1c00c5b60e3"><code class="r-1vckr1u r-z2wwpe r-uibjmv r-m2pi6t r-1hvjb8t" data-slate-leaf="true" data-offset-key="987f6d7645fe40e99accc1c00c5b60e3:0">Error.prototype.stack</code></span></span></a><span key="c5d17d6d03a240a8bfd9cc9ed5d267b9"><span offset-key="c5d17d6d03a240a8bfd9cc9ed5d267b9:0"><span slate-zero-width="z">​</span></span></span>

<span key="0e43e87b27f942aeab0f7d57f58372e3"><span offset-key="0e43e87b27f942aeab0f7d57f58372e3:0">A non-standard Mozilla property for a stack trace.</span></span>

# 

<span key="16f3b8fd8718406bb74afd1ce6728cc0"><span offset-key="16f3b8fd8718406bb74afd1ce6728cc0:0">\[Syntax errors round three\]</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="4ff662bc8e27406e9c1f60c14f813989"><span offset-key="4ff662bc8e27406e9c1f60c14f813989:0">Now if you try playing the game through again, you should get more success --- the game should play through absolutely fine, until you end the game, either by guessing the right number, or by running out of guesses.</span></span>

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="ec01c84a68f549feba0dec25e9decdcc"><span offset-key="ec01c84a68f549feba0dec25e9decdcc:0">At that point, the game fails again, and the same error is spat out that we got at the beginning --- "TypeError: resetButton.addeventListener is not a function"! However, this time it's listed as coming from line 94.</span></span>

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="3329674c1078457a8929bb6dddba4e25"><span offset-key="3329674c1078457a8929bb6dddba4e25:0">Looking at line number 94, it is easy to see that we've made the same mistake here. We again just need to change </span>`addeventListener`<span offset-key="3329674c1078457a8929bb6dddba4e25:2"> to </span>`.addEventListener`<span offset-key="3329674c1078457a8929bb6dddba4e25:4">. Do this now.</span></span>

<span key="791dbc0530084445b80a3dbf3ad1916b"><span offset-key="791dbc0530084445b80a3dbf3ad1916b:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

# 

<span key="7948228c0c2b42dfa4dd61c864fc375f"><span offset-key="7948228c0c2b42dfa4dd61c864fc375f:0">\[A logic error\]</span></span>

<span key="1d493b47ccce43c2a41cb4b114eccd7f"><span offset-key="1d493b47ccce43c2a41cb4b114eccd7f:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<img src="https://i.imgur.com/fDXeVIn.png" class="css-9pa8cd" draggable="false" />

<span key="0da8651367c84919ab9e927578ca6fbf"><span offset-key="0da8651367c84919ab9e927578ca6fbf:0">devide</span></span>

<span key="c71a205cfd794073aa0ba761e6ceff87"><span offset-key="c71a205cfd794073aa0ba761e6ceff87:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="19c6c7050623450a8d46c76d71549fb7"><span offset-key="19c6c7050623450a8d46c76d71549fb7:0">At this point, the game should play through fine, however after playing through a few times you'll undoubtedly notice that the "random" number you've got to guess is always 1. Definitely not quite how we want the game to play out!</span></span>

<span key="52eeab35fbc24eff95db8ea3674b414d"><span offset-key="52eeab35fbc24eff95db8ea3674b414d:0">There's definitely a problem in the game logic somewhere --- the game is not returning an error; it just isn't playing right.</span></span>

1.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">1.</span>
    <span key="36915dcc10c54935b6c06d02730073d9"><span offset-key="36915dcc10c54935b6c06d02730073d9:0">Search for the </span>`randomNumber`<span offset-key="36915dcc10c54935b6c06d02730073d9:2"> variable, and the lines where the random number is first set. The instance that stores the random number that we want to guess at the start of the game should be around line number 44:</span></span>

    1

    <span key="bbccb69af9ed47f69b3919e34d71122b"><span offset-key="bbccb69af9ed47f69b3919e34d71122b:0">let randomNumber = Math.floor(Math.random()) + 1;</span></span>

    <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

    Copied!

2.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">2.</span>
    <span key="9d77002a61e54b53b195844c42230dc4"><span offset-key="9d77002a61e54b53b195844c42230dc4:0">And the one that generates the random number before each subsequent game is around line 113:</span></span>

    1

    <span key="73df426f7c4c45988eb5fafbe8635296"><span offset-key="73df426f7c4c45988eb5fafbe8635296:0">randomNumber = Math.floor(Math.random()) + 1;</span></span>

    <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

    Copied!

3.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">3.</span>
    <span key="ab789d5926fb47959f15467716acc4f0"><span offset-key="ab789d5926fb47959f15467716acc4f0:0">To check whether these lines are indeed the problem, let's turn to our friend </span>`console.log()`<span offset-key="ab789d5926fb47959f15467716acc4f0:2"> again --- insert the following line directly below each of the above two lines:</span></span>

    1

    <span key="ba568215cc7d488a830cb3e70f335abc"><span offset-key="ba568215cc7d488a830cb3e70f335abc:0">console.log(randomNumber);</span></span>

    <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

    Copied!

4.  <span class="r-1awozwy r-1nf4jbm r-6koalj r-18u37iz r-gg6oyi r-ubezar r-16dba41 r-135wba7 r-1m04atk r-1pyaxff" contenteditable="false" style="height:24px">4.</span>
    <span key="e9dd424cd9e9425b883e710c67468e58"><span offset-key="e9dd424cd9e9425b883e710c67468e58:0">Save and refresh, then play a few games --- you'll see that </span>`randomNumber`<span offset-key="e9dd424cd9e9425b883e710c67468e58:2"> is equal to 1 at each point where it is logged to the console.</span></span>

<span key="d0f944d9404f4bc5aa6358fd79357b36"><span offset-key="d0f944d9404f4bc5aa6358fd79357b36:0">split</span></span>

# 

<span key="40fcce41a4294eeebfe82cf201f9515e"><span offset-key="40fcce41a4294eeebfe82cf201f9515e:0">\[Working through the logic\]</span></span>

<span key="32b924b66af74398a12a447369aee1e6"><span offset-key="32b924b66af74398a12a447369aee1e6:0">To fix this, let's consider how this line is working. First, we invoke \[</span>`Math.random()`<span offset-key="32b924b66af74398a12a447369aee1e6:2">\]/Math/random), which generates a random decimal number between 0 and 1, e.g. 0.5675493843.</span></span>

1

<span key="cf83863ac15f48859dc95f10067494fe"><span offset-key="cf83863ac15f48859dc95f10067494fe:0">Math.random();</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="2779e5cd1d104bd89ba43360bd967c16"><span offset-key="2779e5cd1d104bd89ba43360bd967c16:0">Next, we pass the result of invoking </span>`Math.random()`<span offset-key="2779e5cd1d104bd89ba43360bd967c16:2"> through \[</span>`Math.floor()`<span offset-key="2779e5cd1d104bd89ba43360bd967c16:4">\]/Math/floor), which rounds the number passed to it down to the nearest whole number. We then add 1 to that result:</span></span>

1

<span key="c25177e1e4d74d1f9186056c7599e9e4"><span offset-key="c25177e1e4d74d1f9186056c7599e9e4:0">Math.floor(Math.random()) + 1;</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="53443308e619460ca749cfc56c41afcf"><span offset-key="53443308e619460ca749cfc56c41afcf:0">Rounding a random decimal number between 0 and 1 down will always return 0, so adding 1 to it will always return 1. We need to multiply the random number by 100 before we round it down. The following would give us a random number between 0 and 99:</span></span>

1

<span key="53563cb6fc1b43e983e63a884e394230"><span offset-key="53563cb6fc1b43e983e63a884e394230:0">Math.floor(Math.random() \* 100);</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="9959a52b78f54cfa804c9d565e8fcf83"><span offset-key="9959a52b78f54cfa804c9d565e8fcf83:0">Hence us wanting to add 1, to give us a random number between 1 and 100:</span></span>

1

<span key="cc8077b4682b4a7cac548e9d1ac93d02"><span offset-key="cc8077b4682b4a7cac548e9d1ac93d02:0">Math.floor(Math.random() \* 100) + 1;</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="a06a6ab228344ac999ad054e6bb67213"><span offset-key="a06a6ab228344ac999ad054e6bb67213:0">Try updating both lines like this, then save and refresh --- the game should now play like we are intending it to!</span></span>

<span key="bacf1cf9c6a747509afbea0fa33ac0b9"><span offset-key="bacf1cf9c6a747509afbea0fa33ac0b9:0">There are other common errors you'll come across in your code. This section highlights most of them.</span></span>

# 

<span key="10a433d0ef1d4582b52de30d244a4e92"><span offset-key="10a433d0ef1d4582b52de30d244a4e92:0">\[SyntaxError: missing ; before statement\]</span></span>

<span key="da369f3aef314623b1ce2d3b15d0f1eb"><span offset-key="da369f3aef314623b1ce2d3b15d0f1eb:0">This error generally means that you have missed a semicolon at the end of one of your lines of code, but it can sometimes be more cryptic. For example, if we change this line inside the </span>`checkGuess()`<span offset-key="da369f3aef314623b1ce2d3b15d0f1eb:2"> function:</span></span>

1

<span key="8c35dfb48cc64e5bb06f17a1e405bdcd"><span offset-key="8c35dfb48cc64e5bb06f17a1e405bdcd:0">let userGuess = Number(guessField.value);</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="251990f1448a4079966a757b9bfb6b33"><span offset-key="251990f1448a4079966a757b9bfb6b33:0">to</span></span>

1

<span key="6ec1242879334ed5b4fd5b244016af87"><span offset-key="6ec1242879334ed5b4fd5b244016af87:0">let userGuess === Number(guessField.value);</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="9985d1b7b82948d18bbcd1a552333bd2"><span offset-key="9985d1b7b82948d18bbcd1a552333bd2:0">It throws this error because it thinks you are trying to do something different. You should make sure that you don't mix up the assignment operator (</span>`=`<span offset-key="9985d1b7b82948d18bbcd1a552333bd2:2">) --- which sets a variable to be equal to a value --- with the strict equality operator (</span>`===`<span offset-key="9985d1b7b82948d18bbcd1a552333bd2:4">), which tests whether one value is equal to another, and returns a </span>`true`<span offset-key="9985d1b7b82948d18bbcd1a552333bd2:6">/</span>`false`<span offset-key="9985d1b7b82948d18bbcd1a552333bd2:8"> result.</span></span>

<span key="f05b97ebddaa4bf1b54f7d9eb87ffc34">**Note:**<span offset-key="f05b97ebddaa4bf1b54f7d9eb87ffc34:1"> See our \[SyntaxError: missing ; before statement\]Reference/Errors/Missing\_semicolon\_before\_statement) reference page for more details about this error.</span></span>

# 

<span key="a3c3b7a29529400592f7fc0b75cd6685"><span offset-key="a3c3b7a29529400592f7fc0b75cd6685:0">\[The program always says you've won, regardless of the guess you enter\]</span></span>

<span key="63d1f112447e438bbfdbcd543647b300"><span offset-key="63d1f112447e438bbfdbcd543647b300:0">This could be another symptom of mixing up the assignment and strict equality operators. For example, if we were to change this line inside </span>`checkGuess()`<span offset-key="63d1f112447e438bbfdbcd543647b300:2">:</span></span>

1

<span key="6c8f45c4bff44ecc8349b4de081684da"><span offset-key="6c8f45c4bff44ecc8349b4de081684da:0">if (userGuess === randomNumber) {</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="b5542a2406e6484d90d079ae2ddc197a"><span offset-key="b5542a2406e6484d90d079ae2ddc197a:0">to</span></span>

1

<span key="bd81c5eb78424e149d53aab4dd89acf3"><span offset-key="bd81c5eb78424e149d53aab4dd89acf3:0">if (userGuess = randomNumber) {</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="51d63bbdd88a451d8dc6d10d1ea31e1e"><span offset-key="51d63bbdd88a451d8dc6d10d1ea31e1e:0">the test would always return </span>`true`<span offset-key="51d63bbdd88a451d8dc6d10d1ea31e1e:2">, causing the program to report that the game has been won. Be careful!</span></span>

<span key="1f45249a43f8463d970118da72552c4e"><span offset-key="1f45249a43f8463d970118da72552c4e:0">\[SyntaxError: missing\]</span></span>

<span key="ef36d1ab7b404bd39b213cee915335e4"><span offset-key="ef36d1ab7b404bd39b213cee915335e4:0">This one is pretty simple --- it generally means that you've missed the closing parenthesis at the end of a function/method call.</span></span>

<span key="f4dc80890505459c826e24b61648942b">**Note:**<span offset-key="f4dc80890505459c826e24b61648942b:1"> See our \[SyntaxError: missing \] reference page for more details about this error.</span></span>

<span key="5367c46be6ba4b66b36fcd7217849735"><span offset-key="5367c46be6ba4b66b36fcd7217849735:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="d38b8849218847e7b1b767b30d813bf0"><span offset-key="d38b8849218847e7b1b767b30d813bf0:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="74ca133741fc4c69ab9ff890a3a33ed1"><span offset-key="74ca133741fc4c69ab9ff890a3a33ed1:0">split</span></span>

# 

<span key="f9af91ea83dc43cd83d089691a669b8f"><span offset-key="f9af91ea83dc43cd83d089691a669b8f:0">\[SyntaxError:\]</span></span>

<span key="aa6f524a952340079c3bcec378997653"><span offset-key="aa6f524a952340079c3bcec378997653:0">This error usually relates to an incorrectly formed JavaScript object, but in this case we managed to get it by changing</span></span>

1

<span key="3d8782e3419b48b5b330f7d55ada348a"><span offset-key="3d8782e3419b48b5b330f7d55ada348a:0">function checkGuess() {</span></span>

1

<span key="8f2f7b41af8441dabfef3383c488cf53"><span offset-key="8f2f7b41af8441dabfef3383c488cf53:0">function checkGuess( {</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="606c8e3d5bdc4b2dbf22ce7633644e46"><span offset-key="606c8e3d5bdc4b2dbf22ce7633644e46:0">This has caused the browser to think that we are trying to pass the contents of the function into the function as an argument. Be careful with those parentheses!</span></span>

## 

<span key="fbfacfc64db34f71a43adfe000db423a"><span offset-key="fbfacfc64db34f71a43adfe000db423a:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="2c860f4f266e42ab8f8cf825cc73663d"><span offset-key="2c860f4f266e42ab8f8cf825cc73663d:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<img src="https://i.imgur.com/fDXeVIn.png" class="css-9pa8cd" draggable="false" />

<span key="2abc805648f94c6f9a024f008ac4ef06"><span offset-key="2abc805648f94c6f9a024f008ac4ef06:0">split</span></span>

# 

<span key="a8378e42740d426e943bba0b0d6d6be7"><span offset-key="a8378e42740d426e943bba0b0d6d6be7:0">\[SyntaxError: missing } after function body\](What\_went\_wrong#syntaxerror\_missing\_after\_function\_body SyntaxError: missing } after function body")</span></span>

<span key="6ad7cfc163fd4e84b0163d3dae20f092"><span offset-key="6ad7cfc163fd4e84b0163d3dae20f092:0">This is easy --- it generally means that you've missed one of your curly braces from a function or conditional structure. We got this error by deleting one of the closing curly braces near the bottom of the </span>`checkGuess()`<span offset-key="6ad7cfc163fd4e84b0163d3dae20f092:2"> function.</span></span>

## 

<span key="f3f18b3d9812470183812b34c9b388ed"><span offset-key="f3f18b3d9812470183812b34c9b388ed:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="5e8ca4374bbe49fc85123ec21b8c94f7"><span offset-key="5e8ca4374bbe49fc85123ec21b8c94f7:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="b2a128f97ec24838b3e9f5eee7f07803"><span offset-key="b2a128f97ec24838b3e9f5eee7f07803:0">split</span></span>

# 

<span key="bd89bf92c9c74ae5b22d515561724f10"><span offset-key="bd89bf92c9c74ae5b22d515561724f10:0">\[SyntaxError:</span></span>

<span key="ef518df147834f14a664411ed17a14e7"><span offset-key="ef518df147834f14a664411ed17a14e7:0">These errors generally mean that you've left off a string value's opening or closing quote mark. In the first error above, </span>*string*<span offset-key="ef518df147834f14a664411ed17a14e7:2"> would be replaced with the unexpected character(s) that the browser found instead of a quote mark at the start of a string. The second error means that the string has not been ended with a quote mark.</span></span>

<span key="9722984633b64733a428f2a615da8ec7"><span offset-key="9722984633b64733a428f2a615da8ec7:0">For all of these errors, think about how we tackled the examples we looked at in the walkthrough. When an error arises, look at the line number you are given, go to that line and see if you can spot what's wrong. Bear in mind that the error is not necessarily going to be on that line, and also that the error might not be caused by the exact same problem we cited above!</span></span>

<span key="9fe2990ab2a74099a469d9d7ad21bbf4">**Note:**<span offset-key="9fe2990ab2a74099a469d9d7ad21bbf4:1"> See our \[SyntaxError: Unexpected token\]Reference/Errors/Unexpected\_token) and \[SyntaxError: unterminated string literal\]Reference/Errors/Unterminated\_string\_literal) reference pages for more details about these errors.</span></span>

<span key="e7b450db5a564c61a63003e5593277e7"><span offset-key="e7b450db5a564c61a63003e5593277e7:0">Error</span>`objects are thrown when runtime errors occur. The`<span offset-key="e7b450db5a564c61a63003e5593277e7:2">Error\` object can also be used as a base object for user-defined exceptions. See below for standard built-in error types.</span></span>

# 

<span key="ee817565d6ce4c4c95f57617d6b4230d"><span offset-key="ee817565d6ce4c4c95f57617d6b4230d:0">\[Throwing a generic error\]</span></span>

<span key="4916f207438d43c38a69ba85b1c28aa7"><span offset-key="4916f207438d43c38a69ba85b1c28aa7:0">Usually you create an </span>`Error`<span offset-key="4916f207438d43c38a69ba85b1c28aa7:2"> object with the intention of raising it using the \[</span>`throw`<span offset-key="4916f207438d43c38a69ba85b1c28aa7:4">\]Reference/Statements/throw) keyword. You can handle the error using the \[</span>`try...catch`<span offset-key="4916f207438d43c38a69ba85b1c28aa7:6">\]Reference/Statements/try...catch) construct:</span></span>

1

<span key="98672f152ff2470597f626e3b9d72b39"><span offset-key="98672f152ff2470597f626e3b9d72b39:0">try {</span></span>

2

<span key="92505a431de346bab5920472076d064e"><span offset-key="92505a431de346bab5920472076d064e:0"> throw new Error('Whoops!')</span></span>

3

<span key="5bb934b2e32d436e9eed037224e4b989"><span offset-key="5bb934b2e32d436e9eed037224e4b989:0">} catch (e) {</span></span>

4

<span key="2f4b6b10107d4b92aa236d9fa0523fe7"><span offset-key="2f4b6b10107d4b92aa236d9fa0523fe7:0"> console.error(e.name + ': ' + e.message)</span></span>

5

<span key="b17d6238d7e34f81b6660c4d38d414ff"><span offset-key="b17d6238d7e34f81b6660c4d38d414ff:0">}</span></span>

<span key="505c8f1917f74cfc907b95310fa17249"><span offset-key="505c8f1917f74cfc907b95310fa17249:0">\[Handling a specific error type\]</span></span>

<span key="4d5f8d770a5c4a8380a444b79dde9b6d"><span offset-key="4d5f8d770a5c4a8380a444b79dde9b6d:0">You can choose to handle only specific error types by testing the error type with the error's \[</span>`constructor`<span offset-key="4d5f8d770a5c4a8380a444b79dde9b6d:2">\]/Object/constructor) property or, if you're writing for modern JavaScript engines, \[</span>`instanceof`<span offset-key="4d5f8d770a5c4a8380a444b79dde9b6d:4">\]Reference/Operators/instanceof) keyword:</span></span>

# 

<span key="7520e276406a4d2bbaba69a973648fff"><span offset-key="7520e276406a4d2bbaba69a973648fff:0">\[Differentiate between similar errors\]</span></span>

<span key="4dc32dc1b39b4a8abbdeb7c8d58e5c43"><span offset-key="4dc32dc1b39b4a8abbdeb7c8d58e5c43:0">Sometimes a block of code can fail for reasons that require different handling, but which throw very similar errors (i.e. with the same type and message).</span></span>

<span key="6bfef2eb38814ce8accde04ec8372d74"><span offset-key="6bfef2eb38814ce8accde04ec8372d74:0">If you don't have control over the original errors that are thrown, one option is to catch them and throw new </span>`Error`<span offset-key="6bfef2eb38814ce8accde04ec8372d74:2"> objects that have more specific messages. The original error should be passed to the new </span>`Error`<span offset-key="6bfef2eb38814ce8accde04ec8372d74:4"> in the constructor </span>`option`<span offset-key="6bfef2eb38814ce8accde04ec8372d74:6"> parameter (</span>`cause`<span offset-key="6bfef2eb38814ce8accde04ec8372d74:8"> property), as this ensures that the original error and stack trace are available to higher level try/catch blocks.</span></span>

<span key="b8fc554419fd4e07a55faba8c28afd63"><span offset-key="b8fc554419fd4e07a55faba8c28afd63:0">The example below shows this for two methods that would otherwise fail with similar errors (</span>`doFailSomeWay()`<span offset-key="b8fc554419fd4e07a55faba8c28afd63:2"> and </span>`doFailAnotherWay()`<span offset-key="b8fc554419fd4e07a55faba8c28afd63:4">):</span></span>

1

<span key="1e61040045ba49e08daa771f8f099c40"><span offset-key="1e61040045ba49e08daa771f8f099c40:0">function doWork() {</span></span>

2

<span key="1837de106c954f93b3878269c9362446"><span offset-key="1837de106c954f93b3878269c9362446:0"> try {</span></span>

3

<span key="dfbe6f12b73649e8bac26f3a5d392f96"><span offset-key="dfbe6f12b73649e8bac26f3a5d392f96:0"> doFailSomeWay();</span></span>

4

<span key="e066122a227549abb82698746e80fa87"><span offset-key="e066122a227549abb82698746e80fa87:0"> } catch (err) {</span></span>

5

<span key="3c69bbf10adb4d5d9653dadba8478d6f"><span offset-key="3c69bbf10adb4d5d9653dadba8478d6f:0"> throw new Error('Failed in some way', { cause: err });</span></span>

6

<span key="497b049304c3400e8ddf2e694e11a580"><span offset-key="497b049304c3400e8ddf2e694e11a580:0"> }</span></span>

7

<span key="488e0fb668234b0cbef8ff5686fcfbd3"><span offset-key="488e0fb668234b0cbef8ff5686fcfbd3:0"> try {</span></span>

8

<span key="5d9a5a93ca6d4503b28072789473979d"><span offset-key="5d9a5a93ca6d4503b28072789473979d:0"> doFailAnotherWay();</span></span>

9

<span key="d1bd73edc2ba4cb495f6d4c76db926cd"><span offset-key="d1bd73edc2ba4cb495f6d4c76db926cd:0"> } catch (err) {</span></span>

10

<span key="308130e7ff03489e80bff663be325f94"><span offset-key="308130e7ff03489e80bff663be325f94:0"> throw new Error('Failed in another way', { cause: err });</span></span>

11

<span key="aca230b8c2e942c7ad7b5d6a14d3264c"><span offset-key="aca230b8c2e942c7ad7b5d6a14d3264c:0"> }</span></span>

12

<span key="8737b465c7bb463eb12192fd93cf8aca"><span offset-key="8737b465c7bb463eb12192fd93cf8aca:0">}</span></span>

13

<span key="c3de745b2cf2488d95767b268badcf7c"><span offset-key="c3de745b2cf2488d95767b268badcf7c:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

14

<span key="c25461da887547adbdda2d30918f52dd"><span offset-key="c25461da887547adbdda2d30918f52dd:0">try {</span></span>

15

<span key="9006c2113354412f81b3359bc66df7ad"><span offset-key="9006c2113354412f81b3359bc66df7ad:0"> doWork();</span></span>

16

<span key="f11db24fbb344c10b18a67c4fdb5bb79"><span offset-key="f11db24fbb344c10b18a67c4fdb5bb79:0">} catch (err) {</span></span>

17

<span key="0bf9744a3bde434aa1a35a773cbb4aeb"><span offset-key="0bf9744a3bde434aa1a35a773cbb4aeb:0"> switch(err.message) {</span></span>

18

<span key="88ad4f47d3614b609c1eea3571416490"><span offset-key="88ad4f47d3614b609c1eea3571416490:0"> case 'Failed in some way':</span></span>

19

<span key="55deab318a94411b8c4afc2042dd5d4b"><span offset-key="55deab318a94411b8c4afc2042dd5d4b:0"> handleFailSomeWay(err.cause);</span></span>

20

<span key="26d228cb1c874af99bc78eb0f0fe3a4a"><span offset-key="26d228cb1c874af99bc78eb0f0fe3a4a:0"> break;</span></span>

21

<span key="715faaafee5541d3965cd921caf577fa"><span offset-key="715faaafee5541d3965cd921caf577fa:0"> case 'Failed in another way':</span></span>

<span key="6d0eedcb4c1f4867ab442acfa39b5133"><span offset-key="6d0eedcb4c1f4867ab442acfa39b5133:0"> handleFailAnotherWay(err.cause);</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

<span key="13c2dc9ff6ef41c787efaf0a18c23588"><span offset-key="13c2dc9ff6ef41c787efaf0a18c23588:0">You can also use the </span>`cause`<span offset-key="13c2dc9ff6ef41c787efaf0a18c23588:2"> property in \[custom error types\]/error#custom\_error\_types), provided the subclasses' constructor passes the </span>`options`<span offset-key="13c2dc9ff6ef41c787efaf0a18c23588:4"> parameter when calling </span>`super()`<span offset-key="13c2dc9ff6ef41c787efaf0a18c23588:6">:</span></span>

1

# 

<span key="8fbd758fce74440bb481a6ed3ed7869a"><span offset-key="8fbd758fce74440bb481a6ed3ed7869a:0">\[Custom Error Types\]</span></span>

<span key="4f81565bd42e4f9ba46b69d41465fae8"><span offset-key="4f81565bd42e4f9ba46b69d41465fae8:0">You might want to define your own error types deriving from </span>`Error`<span offset-key="4f81565bd42e4f9ba46b69d41465fae8:2"> to be able to </span>`throw new MyError()`<span offset-key="4f81565bd42e4f9ba46b69d41465fae8:4"> and use </span>`instanceof MyError`<span offset-key="4f81565bd42e4f9ba46b69d41465fae8:6"> to check the kind of error in the exception handler. This results in cleaner and more consistent error handling code.</span></span>

<span key="2e71537289c64eccba68e0101bef558f"><span offset-key="2e71537289c64eccba68e0101bef558f:0">See </span></span><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/1382107/whats-a-good-way-to-extend-error-in-javascript" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="c149df52f8a7428eab230091d2370dfb" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="5abf40b7936c4676b58fd760993da4e3"><span data-offset-key="5abf40b7936c4676b58fd760993da4e3:0">"What's a good way to extend Error in JavaScript?"</span></span></span></a><span key="9a258d0deb02437493524e57e5d31a44"><span offset-key="9a258d0deb02437493524e57e5d31a44:0"> on StackOverflow for an in-depth discussion.</span></span>

<img src="https://i.imgur.com/fDXeVIn.png" class="css-9pa8cd" draggable="false" />

<span key="adb9319e6fc54c8aa91e7e6055510bc3"><span offset-key="adb9319e6fc54c8aa91e7e6055510bc3:0">devide</span></span>

<span key="c54c5d149c6243738198074ac186dd06"><span offset-key="c54c5d149c6243738198074ac186dd06:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="415b8102b24e463fba0a78e089e30e79"><span offset-key="415b8102b24e463fba0a78e089e30e79:0">ES6 Custom Error Class</span></span>

<span key="aaeef861d3fd457fba5a20a446386bbf">**Warning:**<span offset-key="aaeef861d3fd457fba5a20a446386bbf:1"> Versions of Babel prior to 7 can handle </span>`CustomError`<span offset-key="aaeef861d3fd457fba5a20a446386bbf:3"> class methods, but only when they are declared with \[Object.defineProperty()\]/Object/defineProperty). Otherwise, old versions of Babel and other transpilers will not correctly handle the following code without </span></span><a href="https://github.com/loganfsmyth/babel-plugin-transform-builtin-extend" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="24870d05805b4d1cbbe41f090a367f57" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="b69cfa67c3584c4e9489620b89977b50"><span data-offset-key="b69cfa67c3584c4e9489620b89977b50:0">additional configuration</span></span></span></a><span key="575387e2811d45178bbee07c828ed3c7"><span offset-key="575387e2811d45178bbee07c828ed3c7:0">.</span></span>

# 

<span key="a7523c4528cc45e4acd70b9f65c32254"><span offset-key="a7523c4528cc45e4acd70b9f65c32254:0">Challenge:</span></span>

<span key="d62c3606dc2f4751b8db8dd85972c73a"><span offset-key="d62c3606dc2f4751b8db8dd85972c73a:0">There is a made up API URL (</span>`http://great.jokes/christmas`<span offset-key="d62c3606dc2f4751b8db8dd85972c73a:2">) that you can call to a get list of Christmas jokes in JSON format.</span></span>

## 

<span key="79fcf2af5f654102a48ba70a2a0e1920"><span offset-key="79fcf2af5f654102a48ba70a2a0e1920:0">Your challenge</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="ccd07397d3524acc8c78ab2f0a7e6a47"><span offset-key="ccd07397d3524acc8c78ab2f0a7e6a47:0">Write an async function which takes an </span>`apiUrl`<span offset-key="ccd07397d3524acc8c78ab2f0a7e6a47:2"> and </span>`jokeId`<span offset-key="ccd07397d3524acc8c78ab2f0a7e6a47:4"> which returns a promise.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="c38e8302badf4c9398f0cf1094e2a942"><span offset-key="c38e8302badf4c9398f0cf1094e2a942:0">The data will need to be filtered to get the specified joke by </span>`id`<span offset-key="c38e8302badf4c9398f0cf1094e2a942:2">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="175ee7a1b0964288bd3514cb43ff8723"><span offset-key="175ee7a1b0964288bd3514cb43ff8723:0">When you got the joke it should be accessible through a simple API of </span>`saySetup`<span offset-key="175ee7a1b0964288bd3514cb43ff8723:2"> and </span>`sayPunchLine`<span offset-key="175ee7a1b0964288bd3514cb43ff8723:4"> methods.</span></span>

<span key="c1f8a7c7eac7450992fd41916ecd6758"><span offset-key="c1f8a7c7eac7450992fd41916ecd6758:0">Handle error cases</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="d707e45243554a6ca7be7ea544f950ff"><span offset-key="d707e45243554a6ca7be7ea544f950ff:0">If a joke can't be found throw an error message in this format </span>`new Error('No jokes found id: {jokeId}')`<span offset-key="d707e45243554a6ca7be7ea544f950ff:2">.</span></span>

-   <img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgOCAxNiIgcHJlc2VydmVhc3BlY3RyYXRpbz0ieE1pZFlNaWQgbWVldCIgY2xhc3M9InItMW5mNGpibSByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJoZWlnaHQ6MTJweDt3aWR0aDoxMnB4Ij48cGF0aCBkPSJNMCA4YzAtMi4yIDEuOC00IDQtNHM0IDEuOCA0IDQtMS44IDQtNCA0LTQtMS44LTQtNHoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIj48L3BhdGg+PC9zdmc+" class="r-1nf4jbm r-1vzi8xi" />

    <span key="ab5500b27b3e46cbab13c0a2cfa1c60e"><span offset-key="ab5500b27b3e46cbab13c0a2cfa1c60e:0">Getting jokes from a another API URL may return a different data shape, throw this error message </span>`new Error('No jokes at url: {url}')`<span offset-key="ab5500b27b3e46cbab13c0a2cfa1c60e:2"> for an unexpected shape.</span></span>

<span key="18058c684ba34a178856541bb9c3f970">*Throw error in a promise style*</span>

## 

<span key="839d9b12dd5141a2bf03ea54a5b94a87"><span offset-key="839d9b12dd5141a2bf03ea54a5b94a87:0">Info</span></span>

<span key="354c8c775b1e42eab682f492ece9787b"><span offset-key="354c8c775b1e42eab682f492ece9787b:0">Get the data using the mocked </span>`fetch(url)`<span offset-key="354c8c775b1e42eab682f492ece9787b:2"> function, which implements the basics of the fetch api. </span></span><a href="https://davidwalsh.name/fetch" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="cca9f1b89b3c469f8685336f3d4a7be6" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="641e96e73208409aa1d83b44cdc5a21f"><span data-offset-key="641e96e73208409aa1d83b44cdc5a21f:0">Learn about fetch</span></span></span></a><span key="da6cd10d7ac8482a895ba8f87593cd5b"><span offset-key="da6cd10d7ac8482a895ba8f87593cd5b:0">. </span></span><a href="https://javascript.info/async-await" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="64dad1a9211c48078a9bdf6ea031a70b" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="6bed457f5a71437eb8c18df660a37403"><span data-offset-key="6bed457f5a71437eb8c18df660a37403:0">Learn about async/await</span></span></span></a><span key="8b6aaddc867b4d549b2a97297c77f59f"><span offset-key="8b6aaddc867b4d549b2a97297c77f59f:0">.</span></span>

<span key="3b32248656994c8da2018765a8ebf977"><span offset-key="3b32248656994c8da2018765a8ebf977:0">Joke data shape:</span></span>

1

<span key="5bf43dbb052c4d328871b4a61a08a53f"><span offset-key="5bf43dbb052c4d328871b4a61a08a53f:0">{</span></span>

2

<span key="c6f516a5042041b2b91192faea58da15"><span offset-key="c6f516a5042041b2b91192faea58da15:0"> jokes: \[{</span></span>

3

<span key="7baa9bad2a4c4c10826f20d25c61366c"><span offset-key="7baa9bad2a4c4c10826f20d25c61366c:0"> id: 101,</span></span>

4

<span key="78a5def1451e4073b8b783dfeb4aea5b"><span offset-key="78a5def1451e4073b8b783dfeb4aea5b:0"> setup: "Who is Santa's favorite singer?",</span></span>

5

<span key="99ad8e36ef5040738d73f02352e3308f"><span offset-key="99ad8e36ef5040738d73f02352e3308f:0"> punchLine: "Elf-is Presley!"</span></span>

6

<span key="166a025d89524fa59702180fb789595b"><span offset-key="166a025d89524fa59702180fb789595b:0"> },</span></span>

7

<span key="d50a0557b17a44ce8066c375c8868b95"><span offset-key="d50a0557b17a44ce8066c375c8868b95:0">...moreJokes\]</span></span>

8

<span key="cf1fe31a98364f34a970920d1b68b2da"><span offset-key="cf1fe31a98364f34a970920d1b68b2da:0">// Use for your tests ^^</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="40f36df69c6b4cac9d1e4986249d0c41"><span offset-key="40f36df69c6b4cac9d1e4986249d0c41:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="c256102e971941ba9aa01ba7cac1c9be"><span offset-key="c256102e971941ba9aa01ba7cac1c9be:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="c2f5e5701fa14d4d9cab6ca0e3df28bb"><span offset-key="c2f5e5701fa14d4d9cab6ca0e3df28bb:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="860a6b09db3d43fb85579edaf1632a69"><span offset-key="860a6b09db3d43fb85579edaf1632a69:0"><span slate-zero-width="n">​</span></span></span>

<span key="d79b71a6dccb4e05a1ae0933a935a347"><span offset-key="d79b71a6dccb4e05a1ae0933a935a347:0">239</span></span>

<span key="3cc1c657490045e3aae3180e4920c9b5"><span offset-key="3cc1c657490045e3aae3180e4920c9b5:0">The only standard field Error object has is the message property. (See MDN, or EcmaScript Language Specification, section 15.11) Everything else is platform specific.</span></span>

<span key="031a1feff64c4d49b0b165e642301f40"><span offset-key="031a1feff64c4d49b0b165e642301f40:0">Mosts environments set the stack property, but fileName and lineNumber are practically useless to be used in inheritance.</span></span>

<span key="afe706f33bbf4c63b02f7c3fab4f148e"><span offset-key="afe706f33bbf4c63b02f7c3fab4f148e:0">So, the minimalistic approach is:</span></span>

<span key="05ec9220cf1e4f8e92320f2a2e690421"><span offset-key="05ec9220cf1e4f8e92320f2a2e690421:0">function MyError(message) { </span></span><a href="http://this.name" class="css-4rbku5 css-1dbjc4n r-1loqt21 r-1471scf r-1otgn73 r-1i6wzkk r-lrvibr"><span data-key="f5d29441c52244b99bcdd03cbe9d98ca" data-rnw-int-class="nearest_260-2678_262-2679-240__"><span data-key="8bc09b6cbe714004ad0b64a94754e179"><span data-offset-key="8bc09b6cbe714004ad0b64a94754e179:0">this.name</span></span></span></a><span key="1e1fe4b1f04f4475a809f397f122cd46"><span offset-key="1e1fe4b1f04f4475a809f397f122cd46:0"> = 'MyError'; this.message = message; this.stack = (new Error()).stack; } MyError.prototype = new Error; // &lt;-- remove this if you do not // want MyError to be instanceof Error You could sniff the stack, unshift unwanted elements from it and extract information like fileName and lineNumber, but doing so requires information about the platform JavaScript is currently running upon. Most cases that is unnecessary -- and you can do it in post-mortem if you really want.</span></span>

<span key="417674e6e9c640258176c76f23fb7cd5"><span offset-key="417674e6e9c640258176c76f23fb7cd5:0">Safari is a notable exception. There is no stack property, but the throw keyword sets sourceURL and line properties of the object that is being thrown. Those things are guaranteed to be correct.</span></span>

## 

<span key="4a9281224f804d9cbd4dbcaec8fcb1f6"><span offset-key="4a9281224f804d9cbd4dbcaec8fcb1f6:0">1. Lint JavaScript by configuring and running ESLint</span></span>

1

<span key="965ce8fd80b8462193ecbd7b3911f890"><span offset-key="965ce8fd80b8462193ecbd7b3911f890:0">$ npm run lint</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="ad9b4bd2e69e4472914d05ba892681a7"><span offset-key="ad9b4bd2e69e4472914d05ba892681a7:0">Eslint rules with </span>`error`<span offset-key="ad9b4bd2e69e4472914d05ba892681a7:2"> will exit the process and fail a build.</span></span>

<span key="4326577395dc4e3c8345e2ba39d88386"><span offset-key="4326577395dc4e3c8345e2ba39d88386:0">Eslint rules with </span>`warn`<span offset-key="4326577395dc4e3c8345e2ba39d88386:2"> will continue to run the process and not fail a build.</span></span>

<span key="e0aa433bb85f4e03abda4586f6299585"><span offset-key="e0aa433bb85f4e03abda4586f6299585:0">Eslint rules with </span>`off`<span offset-key="e0aa433bb85f4e03abda4586f6299585:2"> will ignore the rule entirely.</span></span>

<span key="6fc798feea974ed284e9ba3f80f853bc"><span offset-key="6fc798feea974ed284e9ba3f80f853bc:0">One can extend one's eslint config using the </span>`extends`<span offset-key="6fc798feea974ed284e9ba3f80f853bc:2"> property. </span>`eslint:recommended`<span offset-key="6fc798feea974ed284e9ba3f80f853bc:4"> is a built-in config.</span></span>

<span key="6f9b4171d2ee4d6f81ada70d8ffcc01d"><span offset-key="6f9b4171d2ee4d6f81ada70d8ffcc01d:0">The </span>`env`<span offset-key="6f9b4171d2ee4d6f81ada70d8ffcc01d:2"> property can be used to set the environment against which files should be evaluated.</span></span>

## 

<span key="54d9cdbae521418196162d834381700b"><span offset-key="54d9cdbae521418196162d834381700b:0">2. Format Code by installing and running Prettier</span></span>

<span key="e56d7ca450104538ab8541a6ef483ef5">`prettier`<span offset-key="e56d7ca450104538ab8541a6ef483ef5:1"> can be used to format code in files via CLI:</span></span>

1

<span key="44632f9f0e2e42ec965ce96482300095"><span offset-key="44632f9f0e2e42ec965ce96482300095:0">$ prettier --write path/to/files</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

<span key="91a8157d545842d1942b3fab8430f96c">`prettier`<span offset-key="91a8157d545842d1942b3fab8430f96c:1"> can be used to format markdown and graphql, too.</span></span>

## 

<span key="9d5c590d1b5f4a1c8e00f0b8bd429575"><span offset-key="9d5c590d1b5f4a1c8e00f0b8bd429575:0">3. Configure Prettier</span></span>

<span key="23c3a7b865ea40fb89a8c208242cd22e">`prettier`<span offset-key="23c3a7b865ea40fb89a8c208242cd22e:1"> allows for a </span>`.prettierignore`<span offset-key="23c3a7b865ea40fb89a8c208242cd22e:3"> to ignore formatting of generated files</span></span>

## 

<span key="e2bcd36d2842466baf316c7290aedf19"><span offset-key="e2bcd36d2842466baf316c7290aedf19:0">4. Disable Unnecessary ESLint Stylistic Rules with eslint-config-prettier</span></span>

<span key="01e615a1981547349739c42ac438127d">`extend`<span offset-key="01e615a1981547349739c42ac438127d:1">ed eslint configs take precedence from the end of the array.</span></span>

<span key="9a2002d3ebbb48609898347badd25ced">`rules`<span offset-key="9a2002d3ebbb48609898347badd25ced:1"> in the the eslint config take precedence over any extensions.</span></span>

## 

<span key="6d02b4165d6249aaa9b4c6b85f931ea9"><span offset-key="6d02b4165d6249aaa9b4c6b85f931ea9:0">5. Validate all files are formatted when linting</span></span>

<span key="1d4cd150525941b4a37fe1b6e2c9590b">`prettier`<span offset-key="1d4cd150525941b4a37fe1b6e2c9590b:1"> can be run with a </span>`--list-different`<span offset-key="1d4cd150525941b4a37fe1b6e2c9590b:3"> flag which exits with a non-zero code if there are any files that are not formatted correctly. This can be used with </span>`ghooks`<span offset-key="1d4cd150525941b4a37fe1b6e2c9590b:5"> to ensure all team members are using </span>`prettier`<span offset-key="1d4cd150525941b4a37fe1b6e2c9590b:7">.</span></span>

<span key="e1bb7596546b4a72a58f0c18912179eb"><span offset-key="e1bb7596546b4a72a58f0c18912179eb:0">npm scripts can forward command line arguments to each other using the </span>`--`<span offset-key="e1bb7596546b4a72a58f0c18912179eb:2"> operator:</span></span>

1

<span key="7f63f77deeb34dc69b3bf982c307ffb8"><span offset-key="7f63f77deeb34dc69b3bf982c307ffb8:0"> ...</span></span>

2

<span key="eb32d2ac0e9648669c4964bcfd099367"><span offset-key="eb32d2ac0e9648669c4964bcfd099367:0"> "scripts": {</span></span>

3

<span key="5109dcca7976495fb8858098f22c9ea8"><span offset-key="5109dcca7976495fb8858098f22c9ea8:0"> "myscript": "some-command",</span></span>

4

<span key="1e1b5a168aa246f9bff6d00b0fd30111"><span offset-key="1e1b5a168aa246f9bff6d00b0fd30111:0"> "myscript:alpha": "npm run myscript -- --some-flag"</span></span>

5

<span key="273daa12a90448588cb2e7da2e413a52"><span offset-key="273daa12a90448588cb2e7da2e413a52:0"> }</span></span>

6

<span key="3e9ccdcc3c984899bc34168f5504fbc1"><span offset-key="3e9ccdcc3c984899bc34168f5504fbc1:0"> ...</span></span>

<img src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIGZpbGw9Im5vbmUiIHByZXNlcnZlYXNwZWN0cmF0aW89InhNaWRZTWlkIG1lZXQiIGRhdGEtcm53LWludC1jbGFzcz0ibmVhcmVzdF9fXzU3OC0yNjgyXyIgY2xhc3M9InItaDdnZG9iIHItMTBwdHVuNyByLTF2emk4eGkiIHN0eWxlPSJ3aWR0aDoxNnB4Ij48cGF0aCBmaWxsLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGNsaXAtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgZD0iTTAgLjVBLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUgMGgxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEuNS41VjRoLTFWMUgxdjloM3YxSC41YS41LjUgMCAwMS0uNS0uNVYuNXoiIGZpbGw9ImN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciI+PC9wYXRoPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNNSA1LjVhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUtLjVoMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLjUuNXYxMGEuNS41IDAgMDEtLjUuNWgtMTBhLjUuNSAwIDAxLS41LS41di0xMHpNNiA2djloOVY2SDZ6IiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiPjwvcGF0aD48L3N2Zz4=" class="r-h7gdob r-10ptun7 r-1vzi8xi" />

Copied!

1

<span key="38d4e6819ebc4ab68c436b4933ef78ab"><span offset-key="38d4e6819ebc4ab68c436b4933ef78ab:0">$ npm run myscript -- --some-flag</span></span>

2
